Direction by the Election Commission of India
No. 99]	
chennai,  thursday,  may   5,  2016	
	
	
	
	
	
Chithirai 22,  Thunmugi, Thiruvalluvar  Aandu – 2047	
DIRECTION BY THE ELECTION COMMISSION OF INDIA
ELECTION COMMISSION’S DIRECTION SPECIFYING THAT THE VOTES AT THE CURRENT GENERAL ELECTIONS 
TO  THE TAMIL NADU LEGISLATIVE ASSEMBLY, 2016 SHALL BE GIVEN AND RECORDED BY MEANS OF 
ELECTRONIC VOTING MACHINES WITH VOTER VERIFIABLE PAPER AUDIT TRAIL SYSTEM (VVPAT)
No.  SRO G-21/2016.
The following Direction of the Election Commission of India, Nirvachan Sadan, Ashoka Road, 
New Delhi-110 001, dated 30th April, 2016 is published:-
No. 576/3/VVPAT/2016/SDR-Vol.I In partial modification of the Commission’s direction No. 576/3/VVPAT/2016/
SDR-Vol.I, dated 21st March 2016, the Commission has directed that printer with drop box in the Constituencies as 
specified by the Commission, in the said Notification shall be used in the Polling Stations of those Constituencies 
as specified in Annexure-1 to this Notification.
(By Order)
	
ANUJ JAIPURIAR,	
	
Secretary,	
	
Election Commission of India.
Secretariat,	
RAJESH LAKHONI,
Chennai-600 009,	
Chief Electoral Officer &
5th May, 2016	
Principal Secretary to Government,	
	
Public (Elections) Department.
